  77: function SentenceRow({
  78:   sentence,
  79:   show_dropped,
  80:   sentence_id,
  81:   hovered_id,
  82:   onSelect,
  83:   pool,
  84: }: {
  85:   sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence;

  92:   const dropped = !sentence.verifier_pass;

  95:   // I-f5-010: T1-conflict HEURISTIC — when ≥2 distinct T1 sources are cited
  96:   // for one sentence, surface a "may conflict — review Inspector" caption.
  97:   // Honest framing per CLAUDE.md §9.4: this is NOT a semantic conflict

 100:     if (!pool || dropped) return false;

 102:     for (const tok of sentence.provenance_tokens) {
 103:       const m = tok.match(/^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):/);
 104:       if (!m) continue;
 105:       const src = pool.sources.find((s) => s.source_id === m[1]);
 106:       if (src && src.tier === "T1") cited_t1.add(m[1]);
 107:     }
 108:     return cited_t1.size >= 2;
 109:   })();
 110: 
 111:   return (
 112:     <li
 113:       data-testid={dropped ? "dropped-sentence" : "kept-sentence"}
 114:       data-sentence-id={sentence_id}
 115:       role="button"
 116:       tabIndex={0}
 117:       onClick={() => onSelect(sentence_id, sentence)}
 118:       onKeyDown={(e) => {
 119:         if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") {
 120:           e.preventDefault();

 141:             >
 142:               {SURFACE_LABEL[surface]}
 143:             </span>

 146:         <span className={cn(dropped ? "" : "text-foreground")}>

 148:         </span>

   1: """VerifiedReport schema for slice 003 (generator + strict-verify).
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_003/architecture_proposal.md` §"verified_report.py".
   4: 
   5: Pure-types module. No I/O, no LLM, no network. Slice 003's
   6: process_generation() consumes an EvidencePool (slice 002 output) and
   7: produces a VerifiedReport, which slice 004 will export as an audit
   8: bundle.
   9: 
  10: Lives in `polaris_graph.generator2` (note the `2`) to keep separation
  11: from heritage `polaris_graph.generator` (multi_section, live_deepseek)
  12: which serves the legacy honest-rebuild pipeline. Coexistence by design
  13: per PLAN.md §4 Heritage Import.
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import uuid
  19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  20: from typing import Literal
  21: 
  22: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator, model_validator
  23: 
  24: 
  25: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  26: # Type literals
  27: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  28: 
  29: SectionStatus = Literal["verified", "regenerated", "dropped"]
  30: """Per-section outcome from strict_verify:
  31: 
  32: - "verified": original generation passed >=verifier_pass_threshold of
  33:   sentences strict-verified
  34: - "regenerated": original failed; regeneration attempt passed
  35: - "dropped": both attempts failed; section excluded from final report
  36: """
  37: 
  38: PipelineVerdict = Literal["success", "abort_no_verified_sections"]
  39: """Top-level verdict per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 4."""
  40: 
  41: AssertionSurface = Literal[
  42:     "prose",
  43:     "table",
  44:     "summary_bullet",
  45:     "limitation",
  46:     "caption",
  47:     "heading",
  48: ]
  49: """Render-surface kind of a verified assertion (I-f5-009).
  50: 
  51: Per Carney plan §F: every assertion-bearing surface in a verified report
  52: must be gated-and-clickable through the Inspector OR explicitly marked
  53: ungated. Today's generator emits only "prose"; future Issues populate
  54: the other 5 surfaces as the generator learns to label table cells,
  55: summary bullets, etc."""
  56: 
  57: DropReason = Literal[
  58:     "invalid_token",       # token doesn't reference a known source_id
  59:     "span_out_of_range",   # span_start > span_end or > len(full_text)
  60:     "numeric_mismatch",    # decimal in sentence not present in cited span
  61:     "overlap_too_low",     # < min_content_overlap shared content words
  62:     "no_provenance_token", # sentence has no [#ev:...:start-end] tokens
  63: ]
  64: 
  65: 
  66: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  67: # VerifiedSentence — atomic verified unit
  68: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  69: 
  70: class VerifiedSentence(BaseModel):
  71:     """A single sentence emitted by the generator after strict-verify.
  72: 
  73:     Sentences that fail strict_verify are still represented here with
  74:     `verifier_pass=False` and a `drop_reason`, so the audit bundle can
  75:     surface "what got proposed and dropped" alongside "what shipped."
  76:     """
  77: 
  78:     section_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
  79:     sentence_text: str = Field(min_length=1)
  80:     provenance_tokens: list[str] = Field(
  81:         default_factory=list,
  82:         description="Token strings of form '[#ev:<source_id>:<start>-<end>]'",
  83:     )
  84:     verifier_pass: bool
  85:     drop_reason: DropReason | None = None
  86:     evaluator_agrees: bool | None = Field(
  87:         default=None,
  88:         description=(
  89:             "Two-family evaluator agreement per CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 1. "
  90:             "True = evaluator confirms generator claim; False = evaluator "
  91:             "disagrees; None = pending (no evaluator pass yet). At rule-based "
  92:             "stage this mirrors verifier_pass; future Issue plugs in the "
  93:             "real two-family LLM judge to populate this independently."
  94:         ),
  95:     )
  96:     assertion_surface: AssertionSurface = Field(
  97:         default="prose",
  98:         description=(
  99:             "Render-surface kind per I-f5-009. Default 'prose' preserves "
 100:             "back-compat with all existing fixtures. Non-prose values are "
 101:             "populated by future generator wiring (table cells, summary "
 102:             "bullets, limitations, captions, headings); the Inspector gates "
 103:             "all six surfaces equally."
 104:         ),
 105:     )
 106:     contradiction: "ContradictionSignal | None" = Field(
 107:         default=None,
 108:         description=(
 109:             "Optional contradiction signal (I-f8-001). When present, "
 110:             "≥2 sources cited for this sentence disagree on the claim. "
 111:             "Default None preserves back-compat. Future Issue (F8-002+) "
 112:             "wires real detection into the generator."
 113:         ),
 114:     )
 115:     is_synthesis_claim: bool = Field(
 116:         default=False,
 117:         description=(
 118:             "True iff sentence is a synthesis claim (e.g., a discussion "
 119:             "paragraph summarizing across sources without quoting any one). "
 120:             "Synthesis claims have no provenance_tokens by definition; "
 121:             "non-synthesis kept sentences MUST have ≥1 provenance token. "
 122:             "Today's generator defaults to False; future Issue may wire the "
 123:             "prompt template to label synthesis sentences explicitly."
 124:         ),
 125:     )
 126: 
 127:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 128:     def _drop_reason_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 129:         if self.verifier_pass is False and self.drop_reason is None:
 130:             raise ValueError(
 131:                 "drop_reason is required when verifier_pass=False"
 132:             )
 133:         if self.verifier_pass is True and self.drop_reason is not None:
 134:             raise ValueError(
 135:                 "drop_reason must be None when verifier_pass=True"
 136:             )
 137:         return self
 138: 
 139:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 140:     def _evaluator_agreement_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 141:         if self.verifier_pass is False and self.evaluator_agrees is True:
 142:             raise ValueError(
 143:                 "evaluator_agrees=True is forbidden when verifier_pass=False "
 144:                 "(rule-based dropped the sentence; evaluator cannot pass it "
 145:                 "without contradicting strict-verify)"
 146:             )
 147:         return self
 148: 
 149:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 150:     def _synthesis_claim_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedSentence":
 151:         if self.is_synthesis_claim and self.verifier_pass is False:
 152:             raise ValueError(
 153:                 "is_synthesis_claim=True requires verifier_pass=True "
 154:                 "(synthesis claims either ship or are dropped before reaching "
 155:                 "this record)"
 156:             )
 157:         if self.is_synthesis_claim and len(self.provenance_tokens) > 0:
 158:             raise ValueError(
 159:                 "is_synthesis_claim=True requires provenance_tokens=[] "
 160:                 "(synthesis claims have no specific provenance — that's the "
 161:                 "definition)"
 162:             )
 163:         if (
 164:             not self.is_synthesis_claim
 165:             and self.verifier_pass is True
 166:             and len(self.provenance_tokens) == 0
 167:         ):
 168:             raise ValueError(
 169:                 "kept non-synthesis sentence requires ≥1 provenance token; "
 170:                 "set is_synthesis_claim=True for prose without specific "
 171:                 "provenance"
 172:             )
 173:         return self
 174:

 177: # FrameCoverage (I-f7-001)
 178: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 179: 
 180: class ContradictionSignal(BaseModel):
 181:     """Inline contradiction annotation per sentence (I-f8-001).
 182: 
 183:     Indicates ≥2 cited sources disagree on the claim in the sentence.
 184:     Future Issue (F8-002+) populates this from real conflict detection;
 185:     today the field is the surface, not the producer."""
 186: 
 187:     disagreeing_source_count: int = Field(ge=2, le=20)
 188:     summary: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=500)
 189: 
 190: 
 191: GapReason = Literal[
 192:     "paywalled",
 193:     "no_oa",
 194:     "source_tier_ineligible",
 195:     "language_unavailable",
 196:     "retracted_only",
 197:     "jurisdiction_outside",
 198:     "not_indexed",
 199:     "embargoed",
 200:     "other",
 201: ]
 202: """Frozen taxonomy of frame-gap reasons (I-f7-002).
 203: 
 204: Replaces the free-text reason from I-f7-001. Forces consistent UI
 205: labels and analytics aggregation. `other` is the escape hatch — paired
 206: with `reason_detail` when it's used."""

 213:     reason: GapReason
 214:     reason_detail: str | None = Field(
 215:         default=None,
 216:         max_length=500,
 217:         description=(
 218:             "Optional free-text supplement to the enum reason "
 219:             "(I-f7-002). Renders as 'Label: detail' in the panel."
 220:         ),
 221:     )
 222:

 224: class FrameCoverage(BaseModel):

 succeeded in 2713ms:
 560:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 561: ): number {
 562:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 563: }
 564: 
 565: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 566: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 567:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 568: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 569:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 570:     T1: 0,
 571:     T2: 1,
 572:     T3: 2,
 573:   };
 574:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 575:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 576:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 577:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 578:   });
 579: }

 255: class Section(BaseModel):
 256:     """A report section (e.g. 'Population', 'Outcomes').
 257: 
 258:     `verified_sentences` includes both passed AND dropped sentences for
 259:     audit completeness; UI filters by `verifier_pass` when rendering the
 260:     user-facing report. `section_verify_pass_rate` is over all attempted
 261:     sentences (not just kept ones).

 267:     section_verify_pass_rate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
 268:     section_status: SectionStatus
 269: 
 270:     def kept_sentences(self) -> list[VerifiedSentence]:
 271:         """Filter to sentences that passed strict_verify."""
 272:         return [s for s in self.verified_sentences if s.verifier_pass]

 329:         started = info.data.get("started_at_utc")
 330:         if started is not None and v < started:
 331:             raise ValueError(
 332:                 "finished_at_utc must be >= started_at_utc"
 333:             )
 334:         return v

 336:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 337:     def _verdict_consistency(self) -> "VerifiedReport":
 338:         """If verdict=success, at least one section must be verified or
 339:         regenerated. If verdict=abort_no_verified_sections, every section
 340:         (if any) must be 'dropped' or sections may be empty."""
 341:         if self.pipeline_verdict == "success":
 342:             kept = [
 343:                 s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"
 344:             ]
 345:             if not kept:
 346:                 raise ValueError(
 347:                     "pipeline_verdict='success' requires at least one "
 348:                     "non-dropped section"
 349:                 )
 350:         else:  # abort_no_verified_sections
 351:             for section in self.sections:
 352:                 if section.section_status != "dropped":
 353:                     raise ValueError(
 354:                         "pipeline_verdict='abort_no_verified_sections' "
 355:                         "requires all sections (if any) to be dropped"
 356:                     )
 357:         return self
 358: 
 359:     def kept_sections(self) -> list[Section]:
 360:         """Filter to non-dropped sections."""
 361:         return [s for s in self.sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]

 181: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 182: # Public orchestrator
 183: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 184: 
 185: def process_generation(
 186:     pool: EvidencePool,
 187:     completion_fn: GeneratorCompletionFn = _default_completion_fn,
 188:     blueprint: Blueprint | None = None,
 189:     verifier_pass_threshold: float = DEFAULT_VERIFIER_PASS_THRESHOLD,
 190:     scope_class: str | None = None,
 191:     generator_model: str = DEFAULT_GENERATOR_MODEL_LABEL,
 192: ) -> VerifiedReport | GenerationError:
 193:     """Run an EvidencePool through generator + strict-verify.
 194: 
 195:     Returns:
 196:         VerifiedReport on either success path or all-sections-dropped abort.
 197:         GenerationError when input pool is structurally invalid OR
 198:             completion_fn is the sentinel default OR raises persistently.
 199:     """
 200:     err = _validate_pool(pool)
 201:     if err is not None:
 202:         return err
 203: 
 204:     started = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 205:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 206: 
 207:     if blueprint is None:
 208:         # scope_class is preferred; falls back to DEFAULT_BLUEPRINT (efficacy)
 209:         # when None. EvidencePool does not currently carry scope_class —
 210:         # callers (e.g. the FastAPI route) must thread it through from the
 211:         # ScopeDecision that triggered retrieval.
 212:         blueprint = blueprint_for_scope_class(scope_class)
 213: 
 214:     # Derive a real generator_model label when the injected completion_fn
 215:     # exposes one (e.g. RealCompletion.model_label). Stub functions used
 216:     # in tests don't have it, so we fall back to the explicit arg.
 217:     effective_model = generator_model
 218:     if generator_model == DEFAULT_GENERATOR_MODEL_LABEL:
 219:         candidate = getattr(completion_fn, "model_label", None)
 220:         if isinstance(candidate, str) and candidate.strip():
 221:             effective_model = candidate
 222: 
 223:     # Generate all sections in parallel. Each section calls the LLM 1-2
 224:     # times (regen on threshold-fail). With 4 sections, parallel reduces
 225:     # latency from ~4-8 LLM calls serial to ~1-2 LLM calls wall-clock.
 226:     sections_by_idx: dict[int, Section] = {}
 227:     fatal_error: GenerationError | None = None
 228: 
 229:     with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(blueprint.sections)) as pool_exec:
 230:         future_to_idx = {
 231:             pool_exec.submit(
 232:                 _generate_and_verify_section,
 233:                 plan,
 234:                 pool,
 235:                 completion_fn,
 236:                 verifier_pass_threshold,
 237:             ): idx
 238:             for idx, plan in enumerate(blueprint.sections)
 239:         }
 240:         for future in as_completed(future_to_idx):
 241:             idx = future_to_idx[future]
 242:             try:
 243:                 sections_by_idx[idx] = future.result()
 244:             except NotImplementedError:
 245:                 fatal_error = GenerationError(
 246:                     code="completion_backend_unavailable",
 247:                     message=(
 248:                         "completion_fn is the sentinel default; inject a real "
 249:                         "fn (PR 7) or test stub"
 250:                     ),
 251:                     pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 252:                     decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 253:                 )
 254:                 break
 255:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
 256:                 fatal_error = GenerationError(
 257:                     code="completion_backend_unavailable",
 258:                     message=f"completion_fn raised {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}",
 259:                     pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 260:                     decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 261:                 )
 262:                 break
 263: 
 264:     if fatal_error is not None:
 265:         return fatal_error
 266: 
 267:     # Preserve blueprint section order
 268:     sections: list[Section] = [
 269:         sections_by_idx[i] for i in range(len(blueprint.sections))
 270:     ]
 271: 
 272:     finished = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 273:     elapsed_ms = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 274: 
 275:     # Aggregate pass rate over ALL sentences (kept + dropped) across non-dropped sections.
 276:     kept_sections = [s for s in sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 277:     if kept_sections:
 278:         total = sum(len(s.verified_sentences) for s in kept_sections)
 279:         passed = sum(
 280:             sum(1 for v in s.verified_sentences if v.verifier_pass)
 281:             for s in kept_sections
 282:         )
 283:         overall_rate = passed / total if total > 0 else 0.0
 284:         pipeline_verdict = "success"
 285:     else:
 286:         # Every section dropped -> abort. For schema validation, we must
 287:         # carry only dropped sections through.
 288:         sections = [s for s in sections if s.section_status == "dropped"]
 289:         overall_rate = 0.0
 290:         pipeline_verdict = "abort_no_verified_sections"
 291: 
 292:     # When verdict=success, the schema requires sections list to contain
 293:     # only non-dropped OR the verdict consistency check fails. Filter:
 294:     if pipeline_verdict == "success":
 295:         sections = kept_sections
 296: 
 297:     return VerifiedReport(
 298:         pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 299:         decision_id=pool.decision_id,
 300:         sections=sections,
 301:         overall_verify_pass_rate=overall_rate,
 302:         pipeline_verdict=pipeline_verdict,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 303:         generator_model=effective_model,
 304:         evaluator_model="strict_verify_v1",
 305:         family_segregation_passed=True,
 306:         verifier_pass_threshold=verifier_pass_threshold,
 307:         started_at_utc=started,
 308:         finished_at_utc=finished,
 309:         latency_ms=elapsed_ms,
 310:         cost_usd=0.0,
 311:     )

 succeeded in 2156ms:
 380:         section_id="sec_x",
 381:         section_title="X",
 382:         verified_sentences=[_dropped(), _dropped()],
 383:         section_verify_pass_rate=0.0,
 384:         section_status="dropped",
 385:     )
 386:     assert s.section_status == "dropped"

 389: # ---------- VerifiedReport ----------
 390: 
 391: def _success_report(**overrides) -> VerifiedReport:
 392:     started = _now()
 393:     finished = started + timedelta(seconds=10)
 394:     base = dict(
 395:         pool_id="pool-1",
 396:         decision_id="dec-1",
 397:         sections=[
 398:             Section(
 399:                 section_id="sec_population",
 400:                 section_title="Population",

 104:                 "code": "gpg_unavailable",

 108:                 ),

 110:             },
 111:         )
 112: 
 113:     # Build into a temp dir; FileResponse copies it to the wire.
 114:     tmp_dir = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="polaris_audit_"))
 115:     try:
 116:         bundle_path = build_audit_bundle(
 117:             req.decision,
 118:             req.pool,
 119:             req.report,
 120:             output_dir=tmp_dir,
 121:             sign_fn=sign_fn,
 122:         )
 123:     except ValueError as exc:
 124:         # FK chain mismatch, verdict != success, cited-span unreachable, or copyrighted span
 125:         msg = str(exc)
 126:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 127:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 128:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 129:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 130:         elif "FK chain" in msg or "pool_id" in msg or "decision_id" in msg:

 succeeded in 3237ms:
   1: """Real OpenRouter-backed completion_fn for slice 003 generator.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_003/architecture_proposal.md` PR 7 row.
   4: 
   5: Implements GeneratorCompletionFn protocol with an OpenRouter chat-completion
   6: backend. Default model from OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL env var (e.g.
   7: 'z-ai/glm-5.1'). Prompt template instructs the LLM to:
   8: 
   9:   - write 4-8 sentences for the requested section
  10:   - cite EVERY claim with a [#ev:<source_id>:<start>-<end>] token
  11:   - never invent decimal numbers — only cite numbers that appear in
  12:     the cited span
  13:   - use only the supplied evidence; do not invoke external knowledge
  14: 
  15: Strict-verify (slice 003 PR 4) drops sentences that violate these rules
  16: post-generation, so the LLM occasionally producing bad output is OK —
  17: the gate enforces the contract regardless.
  18: 
  19: Fail-loud per LAW II:
  20:   - OPENROUTER_API_KEY missing → RuntimeError at construction
  21:   - OpenRouter returns malformed JSON → propagate exception
  22:   - HTTP errors → propagate (orchestrator catches, returns
  23:     GenerationError(completion_backend_unavailable))
  24: """
  25: 
  26: from __future__ import annotations
  27: 
  28: import logging
  29: import os
  30: from dataclasses import dataclass
  31: from typing import Any
  32: 
  33: import httpx
  34: 
  35: from polaris_graph.generator2.section_blueprint import SectionPlan
  36: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  37: 
  38: _LOG = logging.getLogger(__name__)
  39: 
  40: OPENROUTER_ENDPOINT = "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions"
  41: DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_S = 60.0
  42: DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE = 0.2
  43: DEFAULT_MAX_TOKENS = 800
  44: 
  45: # Cap evidence excerpts in the prompt to keep total tokens manageable.
  46: # Each source contributes its first MAX_EVIDENCE_CHARS_PER_SOURCE chars.
  47: MAX_EVIDENCE_CHARS_PER_SOURCE = 800
  48: MAX_SOURCES_IN_PROMPT = 8
  49: 
  50: 
  51: @dataclass
  52: class RealCompletionConfig:
  53:     api_key: str
  54:     model: str
  55:     timeout_s: float = DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_S
  56:     temperature: float = DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE
  57:     max_tokens: int = DEFAULT_MAX_TOKENS
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def load_config_from_env() -> RealCompletionConfig:
  61:     """Build a RealCompletionConfig from environment variables.
  62: 
  63:     Raises RuntimeError if OPENROUTER_API_KEY is unset (fail loud).
  64:     """
  65:     key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY", "").strip()
  66:     if not key:
  67:         raise RuntimeError(
  68:             "OPENROUTER_API_KEY is required for slice 003 real_completion. "
  69:             "Set it in .env before mounting the generation route. Per "
  70:             "CLAUDE.md LAW II, this MUST fail loudly rather than silently "
  71:             "skipping the generator."
  72:         )
  73:     model = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL", "").strip() or "z-ai/glm-5.1"
  74:     return RealCompletionConfig(api_key=key, model=model)
  75: 
  76: 
  77: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  78: # Prompt construction
  79: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  80: 
  81: def _format_evidence_block(pool: EvidencePool) -> str:
  82:     """Build the evidence block of the prompt.
  83: 
  84:     Lists each source with its source_id, tier, title, and a bounded
  85:     excerpt of its full_text (or snippet). The LLM uses these to cite.
  86:     """
  87:     lines: list[str] = []
  88:     sources_used = pool.sources[:MAX_SOURCES_IN_PROMPT]
  89:     for source in sources_used:
  90:         text = source.full_text if source.full_text is not None else source.snippet
  91:         excerpt = text[:MAX_EVIDENCE_CHARS_PER_SOURCE]
  92:         lines.append(
  93:             f"--- source_id: {source.source_id} | tier: {source.tier.value} | "
  94:             f"title: {source.title}\n{excerpt}"
  95:         )
  96:     return "\n\n".join(lines)
  97: 
  98: 
  99: SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a clinical research synthesis engine. Your output is the section text ONLY — no preamble, no meta-commentary, no markdown, no thinking-aloud.
 100: 
 101: RULES (mandatory):
 102: 
 103: 1. Write 4-8 well-formed declarative sentences for the requested section.
 104: 2. EVERY sentence ends with at least one provenance token of the form
 105:    [#ev:<source_id>:<start>-<end>]. source_id MUST be one of the sources
 106:    provided. start/end are character offsets into that source's text.
 107: 3. NEVER invent numbers. Only cite numeric claims (percentages, sample
 108:    sizes, hazard ratios, etc.) that literally appear in the cited span.
 109: 4. NEVER use external knowledge. Use ONLY the supplied evidence excerpts.
 110: 5. NEVER write meta-commentary like "We need to write...", "The
 111:    evidence shows...", "Let me examine...", "I need to...". Skip directly
 112:    to the section content.
 113: 6. If the evidence does not support a claim, say so explicitly with a
 114:    citation to the source that demonstrates the gap.
 115: 
 116: EXAMPLE (for a 'Population' section about aspirin in migraine):
 117: 
 118: INPUT EVIDENCE:
 119: --- source_id: src-A | tier: T1 | title: Cochrane review on aspirin for migraine
 120: The review included 13 trials enrolling 4222 adults aged 18 to 65 years with episodic migraine. Mean age was 38.7 years; 73% were female.
 121: 
 122: OUTPUT (this is the EXACT format expected — note: starts with content,
 123: no preamble, every sentence has a token):
 124: The review included 13 trials enrolling 4222 adults aged 18 to 65 years with episodic migraine [#ev:src-A:0-99]. The cohort had a mean age of 38.7 years and was 73% female [#ev:src-A:101-148].
 125: 
 126: END EXAMPLE.
 127: 
 128: Now produce the section. Output the prose directly with no preamble."""
 129: 
 130: 
 131: def _build_user_prompt(section_plan: SectionPlan, pool: EvidencePool) -> str:
 132:     evidence_block = _format_evidence_block(pool)
 133:     return (
 134:         f"Section to write: {section_plan.section_title}\n\n"
 135:         f"Section guidance: {section_plan.section_brief}\n\n"
 136:         f"Available evidence:\n{evidence_block}\n\n"
 137:         f"Write the section now. Remember: every sentence ends with at "
 138:         f"least one [#ev:source_id:start-end] token; never invent numbers."
 139:     )
 140: 
 141: 
 142: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 143: # Completion function
 144: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 145: 
 146: @dataclass
 147: class RealCompletion:
 148:     """Stateful GeneratorCompletionFn impl backed by OpenRouter chat API."""
 149: 
 150:     config: RealCompletionConfig
 151: 
 152:     @property
 153:     def model_label(self) -> str:
 154:         """Returns the actual model id used for completions.
 155: 
 156:         The generator orchestrator pulls this so VerifiedReport.generator_model
 157:         reflects the live model rather than the 'stub-generator' default.
 158:         """
 159:         return self.config.model
 160: 
 161:     def __call__(
 162:         self,
 163:         prompt: str,
 164:         section_plan: SectionPlan,
 165:         pool: EvidencePool,
 166:     ) -> str:
 167:         # `prompt` is the section_brief; we re-build a richer user prompt
 168:         # with the actual evidence block. Section_plan + pool are the
 169:         # authoritative inputs.
 170:         user_prompt = _build_user_prompt(section_plan, pool)
 171: 
 172:         body = {
 173:             "model": self.config.model,
 174:             "messages": [
 175:                 {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
 176:                 {"role": "user", "content": user_prompt},
 177:             ],
 178:             "temperature": self.config.temperature,
 179:             "max_tokens": self.config.max_tokens,
 180:         }
 181:         headers = {
 182:             "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.config.api_key}",
 183:             "Content-Type": "application/json",
 184:             # OpenRouter recommends these for routing analytics:
 185:             "HTTP-Referer": "https://polaris-canada.local",
 186:             "X-Title": "POLARIS Slice 003 Generator",
 187:         }
 188: 
 189:         with httpx.Client() as client:
 190:             response = client.post(
 191:                 OPENROUTER_ENDPOINT,
 192:                 json=body,
 193:                 headers=headers,
 194:                 timeout=self.config.timeout_s,
 195:             )
 196:             response.raise_for_status()
 197:             data = response.json()
 198: 
 199:         text = _extract_text(data)
 200:         if not text.strip():
 201:             raise RuntimeError(
 202:                 f"OpenRouter returned empty content for section "
 203:                 f"{section_plan.section_id!r}; model={self.config.model!r}"
 204:             )
 205:         return text
 206: 
 207: 
 208: def _extract_text(response_json: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
 209:     """Parse OpenRouter chat-completion response to plain text.
 210: 
 211:     Handles both shapes seen in the wild:
 212:         # Standard string content (most models)
 213:         {"choices": [{"message": {"content": "Generated text..."}}]}
 214: 
 215:         # Multipart content (some Anthropic, Google, etc.)
 216:         {"choices": [{"message": {"content": [
 217:             {"type": "text", "text": "Generated text..."}
 218:         ]}}]}
 219: 
 220:     Falls back to `message.reasoning` when `content` is empty/None and
 221:     reasoning is populated (some routes return reasoning + empty content
 222:     when the model hits a refusal-like state but still produced thought).
 223:     Last-resort: raises RuntimeError so the orchestrator surfaces a
 224:     structured GenerationError.
 225:     """
 226:     choices = response_json.get("choices") or []
 227:     if not choices:
 228:         raise RuntimeError(
 229:             f"OpenRouter response missing 'choices': {response_json}"
 230:         )

  33: const STALE_THRESHOLD_DAYS = 730;
  34: 
  35: function isStale(publication_date: string | null): boolean {
  36:   if (!publication_date) return false;
  37:   const t = new Date(publication_date).getTime();
  38:   if (isNaN(t)) return false;
  39:   const age_days = (Date.now() - t) / (24 * 3600 * 1000);
  40:   return age_days > STALE_THRESHOLD_DAYS;
  41: }

  61: function AgreementBadge({
  62:   evaluator_agrees,
  63: }: {
  64:   evaluator_agrees: boolean | null;
  65: }) {
  66:   if (evaluator_agrees === true) {
  67:     return (
  68:       <span
  69:         data-testid="inspector-agree"
  70:         className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full border border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-emerald-700 uppercase dark:text-emerald-300"
  71:         title="Two-family evaluator agrees with generator claim"
  72:       >
  73:         Agree
  74:       </span>
  75:     );
  76:   }
  77:   if (evaluator_agrees === false) {
  78:     return (
  79:       <span
  80:         data-testid="inspector-disagree"
  81:         className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
  82:         title="Two-family evaluator disagrees with generator claim"
  83:       >
  84:         Disagree
  85:       </span>
  86:     );
  87:   }
  88:   return (
  89:     <span
  90:       data-testid="inspector-agree-pending"
  91:       className="border-border bg-muted/40 text-muted-foreground inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest uppercase"
  92:       title="Two-family evaluator pass not yet recorded"
  93:     >
  94:       Pending
  95:     </span>
  96:   );
  97: }
  98: 
  99: function SpanQuote({
 100:   token,
 101:   text,
 102:   idx,
 103:   spanIdx,
 104: }: {
 105:   token: ParsedToken;
 106:   text: string;
 107:   idx: number;
 108:   spanIdx: number;
 109: }) {
 110:   const out_of_range = token.end > text.length;
 111:   const span = out_of_range ? "" : text.slice(token.start, token.end);
 112:   if (out_of_range) {
 113:     return (
 114:       <p
 115:         data-testid={`inspector-span-out-of-range-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 116:         className="text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 117:       >
 118:         (span out of range: {token.start}-{token.end} of {text.length})
 119:       </p>
 120:     );
 121:   }
 122:   return (
 123:     <blockquote
 124:       data-testid={`inspector-span-${idx}-${spanIdx}`}
 125:       className="border-l-2 border-yellow-400 bg-yellow-50 px-2 py-1 italic dark:bg-yellow-900/20"
 126:     >
 127:       {span || "(empty span)"}
 128:     </blockquote>
 129:   );
 130: }
 131: 
 132: function SourceCard({
 133:   tokens,
 134:   source,
 135:   idx,
 136: }: {
 137:   tokens: ParsedToken[];
 138:   source: RetrievalSource | undefined;
 139:   idx: number;
 140: }) {
 141:   const first = tokens[0];
 142:   if (!source) {
 143:     return (
 144:       <div
 145:         data-testid={`inspector-source-missing-${idx}`}
 146:         className="rounded border border-rose-500/40 p-2 text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 147:       >
 148:         Source <code>{first.source_id}</code> not in pool — token {first.raw}.
 149:       </div>
 150:     );
 151:   }
 152:   const text = source.full_text ?? source.snippet ?? "";
 153:   return (
 154:     <div
 155:       data-testid={`inspector-source-${idx}`}
 156:       className="border-border flex flex-col gap-1 rounded border p-2 text-xs"
 157:     >
 158:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
 159:         <a
 160:           data-testid={`inspector-source-url-${idx}`}
 161:           href={source.url}
 162:           target="_blank"
 163:           rel="noopener noreferrer"
 164:           className="text-blue-700 underline dark:text-blue-300"
 165:         >
 166:           {source.domain}
 167:         </a>
 168:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
 169:           {source.full_text_available === false ? (
 170:             <span
 171:               data-testid={`inspector-paywalled-${idx}`}
 172:               title="Source paywalled or full-text unavailable — span cannot be quoted; URL still actionable."
 173:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-amber-700 uppercase dark:text-amber-300"
 174:             >
 175:               Paywalled
 176:             </span>
 177:           ) : null}
 178:           {source.retracted ? (
 179:             <span
 180:               data-testid={`inspector-retracted-${idx}`}
 181:               title="Source retracted post-publication"
 182:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 183:             >
 184:               Retracted
 185:             </span>
 186:           ) : null}
 187:           {isStale(source.publication_date) ? (
 188:             <span
 189:               data-testid={`inspector-stale-${idx}`}
 190:               title="Source >2 years old (per Carney plan §F currency-of-knowledge)"
 191:               className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-amber-500/40 bg-amber-500/10 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium tracking-widest text-amber-700 uppercase dark:text-amber-300"
 192:             >
 193:               Stale &gt;2y
 194:             </span>
 195:           ) : null}
 196:           <span
 197:             data-testid={`inspector-tier-${source.tier}`}
 198:             title={TIER_RATIONALE[source.tier]}
 199:             className={`rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] tracking-widest uppercase ${TIER_TONE[source.tier]}`}
 200:           >
 201:             {source.tier}
 202:           </span>
 203:         </div>
 204:       </div>
 205:       <p
 206:         data-testid={`inspector-trace-${idx}`}
 207:         className="text-muted-foreground"
 208:       >
 209:         <strong className="text-foreground">{source.title}</strong>
 210:         {source.publication_date && <> · {source.publication_date}</>}
 211:         {source.authors[0] && (
 212:           <>
 213:             {" "}
 214:             · {source.authors.slice(0, 2).join(", ")}
 215:             {source.authors.length > 2 ? " et al." : ""}
 216:           </>
 217:         )}
 218:       </p>
 219:       <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
 220:         {tokens.map((tok, j) => (
 221:           <SpanQuote
 222:             key={j}
 223:             token={tok}
 224:             text={text}
 225:             idx={idx}
 226:             spanIdx={j}
 227:           />
 228:         ))}
 229:       </div>
 230:     </div>
 231:   );
 232: }
 233: 
 234: export function SentenceInspector({
 235:   open,
 236:   onOpenChange,
 237:   sentence,
 238:   sentence_id,
 239:   pool,
 240: }: {
 241:   open: boolean;
 242:   onOpenChange: (next: boolean) => void;
 243:   sentence: ReportVerifiedSentence | null;
 244:   sentence_id: string | null;
 245:   pool: EvidencePool | null;
 246: }) {
 247:   const tokens = sentence ? parseAllTokens(sentence.provenance_tokens) : [];
 248:   const pool_index = new Map(pool?.sources.map((s) => [s.source_id, s]) ?? []);
 249:   const grouped: Map<string, ParsedToken[]> = new Map();
 250:   for (const tok of tokens) {
 251:     const arr = grouped.get(tok.source_id) ?? [];
 252:     arr.push(tok);
 253:     grouped.set(tok.source_id, arr);
 254:   }
 255:   const groups = [...grouped.entries()];
 256:   return (
 257:     <Sheet open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
 258:       <SheetContent
 259:         data-testid="sentence-inspector-sheet"
 260:         side="right"
 261:         className="data-[side=right]:w-full data-[side=right]:sm:w-2/5 data-[side=right]:sm:max-w-none"
 262:       >
 263:         <SheetHeader>
 264:           <SheetTitle data-testid="sentence-inspector-id">
 265:             {sentence_id ?? "Sentence inspector"}
 266:           </SheetTitle>
 267:           <SheetDescription>
 268:             Provenance and verification details for the selected sentence.
 269:           </SheetDescription>
 270:         </SheetHeader>
 271:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 px-4 pb-4 text-sm">
 272:           {sentence && (
 273:             <>
 274:               <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
 275:                 <p
 276:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-text"
 277:                   className="text-foreground flex-1"
 278:                 >
 279:                   {sentence.sentence_text}
 280:                 </p>
 281:                 <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-1">
 282:                   <AgreementBadge
 283:                     evaluator_agrees={sentence.evaluator_agrees}
 284:                   />
 285:                   {sentence.is_synthesis_claim ? <SynthesisClaimBadge /> : null}
 286:                 </div>
 287:               </div>
 288:               {tokens.length === 0 ? (
 289:                 <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs italic">
 290:                   No provenance tokens.
 291:                 </p>
 292:               ) : (
 293:                 <div
 294:                   data-testid="inspector-sources"
 295:                   className="flex flex-col gap-2"
 296:                 >
 297:                   {groups.map(([source_id, group_tokens], i) => (
 298:                     <SourceCard
 299:                       key={source_id}
 300:                       tokens={group_tokens}
 301:                       source={pool_index.get(source_id)}
 302:                       idx={i}
 303:                     />
 304:                   ))}
 305:                 </div>
 306:               )}
 307:               {sentence.drop_reason && (
 308:                 <p
 309:                   data-testid="sentence-inspector-drop"
 310:                   className="text-xs tracking-widest text-rose-700 uppercase dark:text-rose-300"
 311:                 >
 312:                   dropped —{" "}
 313:                   {DROP_REASON_LABEL[sentence.drop_reason as DropReason]}
 314:                 </p>
 315:               )}
 316:             </>
 317:           )}
 318:         </div>
 319:       </SheetContent>
 320:     </Sheet>
 321:   );
 322: }

   3: POST /api/generation — accepts an EvidencePool (typically the slice 002
   4: response) and returns a VerifiedReport (HTTP 200) or GenerationError
   5: detail (HTTP 400).
   6: 
   7: Mirrors slice 001 intake_route.py + slice 002 retrieval_route.py.
   8: 
   9: Mount:
  10:     from polaris_graph.api.generation_route import router as generation_router
  11:     app.include_router(generation_router, prefix="/api")

  37:

  39: 
  40: 
  41: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  42: # Dependency: completion_fn injection
  43: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  44: 
  45: def get_completion_fn() -> GeneratorCompletionFn | None:
  46:     """Returns the active completion_fn or None.
  47: 
  48:     None signals process_generation() to use its default sentinel which
  49:     triggers GenerationError(completion_backend_unavailable). Tests
  50:     override this dep; PR 7 will replace the production default with the
  51:     real OpenRouter-backed adapter.
  52:     """
  53:     return None
  54: 
  55: 
  56: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  57: # Request / response models
  58: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  59: 
  60: class GenerationRequest(BaseModel):
  61:     """POST body for /api/generation.
  62: 
  63:     Accepts an EvidencePool verbatim (as returned by /api/retrieval).
  64:     Pydantic re-validates the structure on the way in so a malformed
  65:     pool yields HTTP 422 before the orchestrator runs.
  66: 
  67:     `scope_class` is OPTIONAL but recommended; without it the generator
  68:     falls back to the clinical_efficacy blueprint. Callers chaining
  69:     intake -> retrieval -> generation should thread the slice 001
  70:     ScopeDecision.scope_class through.
  71: 
  72:     `verifier_pass_threshold` overrides the default per-section pass-rate
  73:     threshold (default 0.40). Lower values let weaker sections through
  74:     (useful for early demos); higher values are stricter.
  75:     """
  76: 
  77:     pool: EvidencePool = Field(
  78:         description="EvidencePool from slice 002 retrieval (adequacy=True)"
  79:     )
  80:     scope_class: str | None = Field(
  81:         default=None,
  82:         description=(
  83:             "Optional clinical_* scope class to select the section "
  84:             "blueprint. Defaults to clinical_efficacy when omitted."
  85:         ),
  86:     )
  87:     verifier_pass_threshold: float | None = Field(
  88:         default=None,
  89:         ge=0.0,
  90:         le=1.0,
  91:         description=(
  92:             "Optional override for the per-section strict-verify pass "
  93:             "rate threshold. None -> use orchestrator default (0.40)."
  94:         ),
  95:     )
  96:     contract: EvidenceContract | None = Field(
  97:         default=None,
  98:         description=(
  99:             "Pre-generation Evidence Contract (I-ecg-001). Generation "
 100:             "REFUSES if missing AND POLARIS_REQUIRE_CONTRACT=1 — request "
 101:             "returns HTTP 400 with code 'contract_required'. Default OFF "
 102:             "for legacy callers during migration period; set env=1 in "
 103:             "production once all callers thread the contract."
 104:         ),
 105:     )
 106: 
 107: 
 108: class GenerationErrorResponse(BaseModel):
 109:     """Body returned with HTTP 400 when generation cannot proceed."""
 110: 
 111:     error: bool = True
 112:     code: str
 113:     message: str
 114:     pool_id: str | None = None
 115:     decision_id: str | None = None
 116: 
 117: 
 118: class GenerationSuccessResponse(BaseModel):
 119:     """Body returned with HTTP 200 wrapping a VerifiedReport.
 120: 
 121:     Note: a VerifiedReport with verdict='abort_no_verified_sections' is
 122:     still HTTP 200 (request succeeded; the corpus generated but every
 123:     section failed strict-verify; UI surfaces the abort verdict).
 124:     HTTP 400 is reserved for structural failures: inadequate input pool,
 125:     completion backend down, malformed output.
 126:     """
 127: 
 128:     error: bool = False
 129:     report: dict
 130:     server_time_utc: str
 131: 
 132: 
 133: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 134: # Routes
 135: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 136: 
 137: @router.post("/generation", response_model=None)
 138: def post_generation(
 139:     req: GenerationRequest,
 140:     completion_fn: GeneratorCompletionFn | None = Depends(get_completion_fn),
 141: ) -> GenerationSuccessResponse | GenerationErrorResponse:
 142:     """Run an EvidencePool through generator + strict-verify."""
 143:     import os
 144: 
 145:     require_contract = os.environ.get("POLARIS_REQUIRE_CONTRACT", "0").strip() == "1"
 146:     if require_contract:
 147:         try:
 148:             assert_generation_has_contract(req.contract, report_id=None)
 149:         except ContractRequiredError as exc:
 150:             raise HTTPException(
 151:                 status_code=400,
 152:                 detail={
 153:                     "error": True,
 154:                     "code": "contract_required",
 155:                     "message": str(exc),
 156:                     "pool_id": req.pool.pool_id,
 157:                     "decision_id": req.pool.decision_id,
 158:                 },
 159:             )
 160: 
 161:     kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {"scope_class": req.scope_class}
 162:     if req.verifier_pass_threshold is not None:
 163:         kwargs["verifier_pass_threshold"] = req.verifier_pass_threshold
 164:     if completion_fn is not None:
 165:         kwargs["completion_fn"] = completion_fn
 166:     result = process_generation(req.pool, **kwargs)
 167: 
 168:     if isinstance(result, GenerationError):
 169:         raise HTTPException(
 170:             status_code=400,
 171:             detail={
 172:                 "error": True,
 173:                 "code": result.code,
 174:                 "message": result.message,
 175:                 "pool_id": result.pool_id,
 176:                 "decision_id": result.decision_id,
 177:             },
 178:         )
 179: 
 180:     assert isinstance(result, VerifiedReport)
 181:     if require_contract and req.contract is not None:
 182:         verdict = evaluate_contract(req.contract, req.pool, result)
 183:         if not verdict.passed:
 184:             raise HTTPException(
 185:                 status_code=400,
 186:                 detail={
 187:                     "error": True,
 188:                     "code": "contract_unsatisfied",
 189:                     "message": (
 190:                         f"contract {req.contract.contract_id} unsatisfied: "
 191:                         f"{', '.join(verdict.failures)}"
 192:                     ),
 193:                     "pool_id": req.pool.pool_id,
 194:                     "decision_id": req.pool.decision_id,
 195:                 },
 196:             )
 197:     return GenerationSuccessResponse(
 198:         report=result.model_dump(mode="json"),
 199:         server_time_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
 200:     )

 307: function scope_reason_for(decision: IntakeScopeDecision): string {
 308:   switch (decision.status) {
 309:     case "out_of_scope":
 310:       return "This question is out of scope for POLARIS clinical research.";
 311:     case "refused":
 312:       return "POLARIS refused this question (instruction-override attempt detected).";
 313:     case "ambiguous_needs_clarification":
 314:       return "This question is ambiguous. Clarify on the /intake page first.";
 315:     default:
 316:       return `Cannot generate for status='${decision.status}'.`;
 317:   }

 702: export async function runGeneration(
 703:   pool: EvidencePool,
 704:   scope_class?: string | null,
 705: ): Promise<GenerationSuccessResponse> {
 706:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/generation`, {
 707:     method: "POST",
 708:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 709:     body: JSON.stringify({ pool, scope_class: scope_class ?? null }),
 710:   });
 711: 
 712:   if (response.status === 400) {
 713:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 714:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as GenerationErrorBody | null;
 715:     if (body && body.error) {
 716:       throw new GenerationBadRequestError(body);
 717:     }
 718:   }
 719: 
 720:   return asJsonOrThrow<GenerationSuccessResponse>(response);
 721: }

 754:   code:
 755:     | "fk_chain_mismatch"

 760:     | "sign_failed";

 763: }

 766:   code: AuditBundleErrorBody["code"];

 769:     super(body.message);
 770:     this.name = "AuditBundleError";
 771:     this.code = body.code;
 772:     this.report_id = body.report_id;
 773:   }

 781:  * field set so callers can show specific UX (e.g. "GPG signer not

 143: def _build_stub_completion(spec: dict, pool: EvidencePool):
 144:     state = {"calls": 0}
 145:     template = spec["stub_completion_text"]
 146:     if pool.sources:
 147:         full_text_len = len(pool.sources[0].full_text or "")
 148:         token = f"[#ev:src-1:0-{full_text_len}]"
 149:         text = template.replace("{{TOKEN}}", token)
 150:     else:
 151:         text = template
 152: 
 153:     def fn(prompt, section_plan, pool):
 154:         state["calls"] += 1
 155:         return text
 156: 
 157:     return fn, state

 225:     else:

 105: def _build_inputs_from_spec(spec: dict) -> tuple[ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, VerifiedReport]:
 106:     """Build the BPEI chain inputs from a golden test spec."""
 107:     iso = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 108:     decision = ScopeDecision(

 118:         ],
 119:     )
 120: 
 121:     # Build sources list. For test_001 single source; for test_002 two sources;

 124:     sources: list[Source] = []

 128:                 url=spec["source_url"],

 131:                 title=spec.get("source_title", "Source"),
 132:                 snippet=spec["source_full_text"][:200],
 133:                 full_text=spec["source_full_text"],
 134:                 full_text_available=True,
 135:                 source_id=spec["source_id"],

 137:             )
 138:         )

 140:         sources.append(

 142:                 url=spec["kept_source_url"],
 143:                 domain="nejm.org",
 144:                 tier=SourceTier.T2,

 148:                 full_text_available=True,
 149:                 source_id=spec["kept_source_id"],
 150:                 provenance={"legal_cleared": True},
 151:             )
 152:         )
 153:     if spec.get("dropped_source_id"):
 154:         sources.append(
 155:             Source(
 156:                 url=spec["dropped_source_url"],
 157:                 domain="random-blog.example",
 158:                 tier=SourceTier.T3,
 159:                 title="Dropped",
 160:                 snippet=spec["dropped_source_full_text"][:200],
 161:                 full_text=spec["dropped_source_full_text"],

 165:             )

 167:

 170:         sources.append(

 203:     verdict = spec.get("verdict", "success")

The new template `<button role="radio">` at `dashboard/page.tsx:233-251` carries explicit `type="button"`. **This is critical** — without `type="button"`, a `<button>` inside `<form onSubmit>` defaults to `type="submit"`, which would mean keyboard activation (Space) of a radio fires `onSubmit` prematurely. The dashboard's `onSubmit` runs `createRun(...)` if scope wasn't rejected — premature submit on first Space-press would bypass the scope check the user is meant to consciously trigger. The author got this right. The same `type="button"` discipline holds on the F-25-modified `remove` button (`:333`), the EvidenceTooltip Trigger button (`:33`), and the contradiction pill (`inspector/[runId]/page.tsx:297`).

outputs\audits\continuous\4f20140_audit.md:22:- **C-sec-form-button-default-type (probe 2):** PASS. The new template `<button role="radio">` at `dashboard/page.tsx:233-251` carries explicit `type="button"`. **This is critical** — without `type="button"`, a `<button>` inside `<form onSubmit>` defaults to `type="submit"`, which would mean keyboard activation (Space) of a radio fires `onSubmit` prematurely. The dashboard's `onSubmit` runs `createRun(...)` if scope wasn't rejected — premature submit on first Space-press would bypass the scope check the user is meant to consciously trigger. The author got this right. The same `type="button"` discipline holds on the F-25-modified `remove` button (`:333`), the EvidenceTooltip Trigger button (`:33`), and the contradiction pill (`inspector/[runId]/page.tsx:297`).

 succeeded in 3764ms:
   1: """Bundle builder — end-to-end audit bundle assembler.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"bundle_builder".
   4: 
   5: Pipeline:
   6:     ScopeDecision + EvidencePool + VerifiedReport (verdict=success)
   7:         ↓
   8:     build_manifest_and_files()  -> manifest + content files
   9:         ↓
  10:     serialize_manifest_yaml()    -> manifest.yaml bytes
  11:         ↓
  12:     sign_fn(manifest.yaml)       -> manifest.yaml.asc bytes
  13:         ↓
  14:     pack_tarball()               -> audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz
  15: 
  16: The output tarball:
  17:     audit_<bundle_id>/
  18:       manifest.yaml
  19:       manifest.yaml.asc
  20:       scope_decision.json
  21:       evidence_pool.json
  22:       verified_report.json
  23:       sources/<source_id>.txt   (for each cited source)
  24:       metadata.json
  25: 
  26: External verifiers run:
  27:     tar -xzf audit_<id>.tar.gz
  28:     cd audit_<id>
  29:     gpg --verify manifest.yaml.asc manifest.yaml
  30:     # then re-hash each content file and compare against manifest.files[*].sha256
  31: """
  32: 
  33: from __future__ import annotations
  34: 
  35: import io
  36: import logging
  37: import tarfile
  38: import time
  39: from pathlib import Path
  40: from typing import Callable
  41: 
  42: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.bundle_schema import BundleManifest
  43: from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.manifest_builder import (
  44:     build_manifest_and_files,
  45:     serialize_manifest_yaml,
  46: )
  47: from polaris_graph.generator2.verified_report import VerifiedReport
  48: from polaris_graph.retrieval2.evidence_pool import EvidencePool
  49: from polaris_graph.scope.scope_decision import ScopeDecision
  50: 
  51: _LOG = logging.getLogger(__name__)
  52: 
  53: 
  54: # Type alias for the sign function we accept (Protocol-style duck typing).
  55: # Concrete impl is GPGSigner from gpg_signer.py; tests can pass a stub.
  56: SignFn = Callable[[bytes], bytes]
  57: 
  58: 
  59: def _default_sign_fn(_payload: bytes) -> bytes:
  60:     """Sentinel that refuses to run.
  61: 
  62:     Forces callers to provide a real signer (or test stub). Per LAW II,
  63:     silently writing an unsigned bundle is FORBIDDEN — the audit bundle's
  64:     legal value comes from the signature.
  65:     """
  66:     raise NotImplementedError(
  67:         "no sign_fn injected. The audit bundle MUST be GPG-signed. "
  68:         "Inject a real signer (e.g. GPGSigner from gpg_signer.py) or "
  69:         "a test stub."
  70:     )
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def build_audit_bundle(
  74:     decision: ScopeDecision,
  75:     pool: EvidencePool,
  76:     report: VerifiedReport,
  77:     output_dir: Path,
  78:     sign_fn: SignFn = _default_sign_fn,
  79: ) -> Path:
  80:     """End-to-end: build manifest + sign + pack tarball.
  81: 
  82:     Args:
  83:         decision: slice 001 ScopeDecision
  84:         pool: slice 002 EvidencePool (must match report.pool_id)
  85:         report: slice 003 VerifiedReport (must have verdict=success)
  86:         output_dir: directory where audit_<id>.tar.gz is written
  87:         sign_fn: function that takes manifest.yaml bytes and returns
  88:                  .asc bytes. Default raises NotImplementedError; callers
  89:                  MUST inject a real signer.
  90: 
  91:     Returns:
  92:         Path to the generated audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz file.
  93: 
  94:     Raises:
  95:         ValueError: if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success' or pool/report
  96:                     FK chain inconsistent.
  97:         RuntimeError: if sign_fn raises (propagated, original error chained).
  98:     """
  99:     if report.pool_id != pool.pool_id:
 100:         raise ValueError(
 101:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.pool_id={report.pool_id!r} != "
 102:             f"pool.pool_id={pool.pool_id!r}"
 103:         )
 104:     if report.decision_id != decision.decision_id:
 105:         raise ValueError(
 106:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.decision_id={report.decision_id!r}"
 107:             f" != decision.decision_id={decision.decision_id!r}"
 108:         )
 109: 
 110:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 111:     manifest, content_files = build_manifest_and_files(decision, pool, report)
 112: 
 113:     manifest_yaml = serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest)
 114: 
 115:     try:
 116:         manifest_sig = sign_fn(manifest_yaml)
 117:     except NotImplementedError:
 118:         raise RuntimeError(
 119:             "audit bundle requires a sign_fn; default sentinel forbids "
 120:             "shipping unsigned bundles per CLAUDE.md LAW II"
 121:         )
 122:     except Exception as exc:
 123:         raise RuntimeError(
 124:             f"sign_fn raised {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 125:         ) from exc
 126: 
 127:     # Pack everything into a single .tar.gz under top-level dir audit_<id>
 128:     output_dir = Path(output_dir)
 129:     output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 130:     bundle_filename = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}.tar.gz"
 131:     bundle_path = output_dir / bundle_filename
 132: 
 133:     with tarfile.open(bundle_path, "w:gz") as tar:
 134:         top_dir = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}"
 135: 
 136:         # 1. manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc (NOT in manifest.files;
 137:         #    they are the manifest itself + signature)
 138:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml", manifest_yaml)
 139:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml.asc", manifest_sig)
 140:

  60:         sources=list(sources),
  61:         adequacy=AdequacyVerdict(
  62:             is_adequate=True,
  63:             sources_per_tier={SourceTier.T1: 0, SourceTier.T2: 0, SourceTier.T3: 0},
  64:             min_required_per_tier={SourceTier.T1: 0, SourceTier.T2: 0, SourceTier.T3: 0},
  65:         ),
  66:         retrieval_started_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  67:         retrieval_finished_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  68:         latency_ms=0,
  69:         cost_usd=0.0,
  70:     )
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def _decision() -> ScopeDecision:
  74:     return ScopeDecision(
  75:         decision_id="dec-1",
  76:         status="in_scope",
  77:         scope_class="clinical_efficacy",
  78:         ambiguity_axes=[
  79:             AmbiguityAxis(
  80:                 axis="population",
  81:                 plausible_interpretations=["adults"],
  82:                 needs_clarification=False,
  83:             )
  84:         ],
  85:     )
  86: 
  87: 
  88: def _report(
  89:     pool_id: str = "pool-1",
  90:     report_id: str | None = None,
  91:     verdict: str = "success",
  92: ) -> VerifiedReport:
  93:     section = Section(
  94:         section_id="sec_x",
  95:         section_title="X",
  96:         verified_sentences=[
  97:             VerifiedSentence(
  98:                 section_id="sec_x",
  99:                 sentence_text="claim [#ev:src-A:0-3].",
 100:                 provenance_tokens=["[#ev:src-A:0-3]"],
 101:                 verifier_pass=True,
 102:             )
 103:         ],
 104:         section_verify_pass_rate=1.0,
 105:         section_status="verified",
 106:     )
 107:     kwargs = dict(
 108:         pool_id=pool_id,
 109:         decision_id="dec-1",
 110:         sections=[section] if verdict == "success" else [],
 111:         overall_verify_pass_rate=1.0 if verdict == "success" else 0.0,
 112:         pipeline_verdict=verdict,
 113:         generator_model="deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro",
 114:         evaluator_model="strict_verify_v1",
 115:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 116:         started_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 117:         finished_at_utc=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 118:         latency_ms=0,
 119:         cost_usd=0.0,
 120:     )
 121:     if report_id is not None:
 122:         kwargs["report_id"] = report_id
 123:     return VerifiedReport(**kwargs)  # type: ignore[arg-type]

  56: def _sha256_bytes(data: bytes) -> str:
  57:     return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def _serialize_json_canonical(model: Any) -> bytes:
  61:     """Pydantic model -> deterministic UTF-8 JSON bytes.
  62: 
  63:     sort_keys + no extra whitespace beyond standard separators ensures
  64:     re-serialization on the verifier side produces identical bytes →
  65:     SHA256 stable across implementations.
  66:     """
  67:     if hasattr(model, "model_dump"):
  68:         payload = model.model_dump(mode="json")
  69:     else:
  70:         payload = model
  71:     return json.dumps(
  72:         payload,
  73:         sort_keys=True,
  74:         ensure_ascii=False,
  75:         separators=(",", ":"),
  76:     ).encode("utf-8")
  77:

  79: def _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report: VerifiedReport, snapshots: dict) -> None:
  80:     """Raise ValueError if any cited span exceeds its snapshot's reachable_chars.
  81: 
  82:     Validates the UNION of tokens parsed from `sentence.sentence_text` and

  84:     unreachable. Span end > reachable_chars => unreachable.
  85:     """
  86:     seen: set[str] = set()
  87:     for section in report.sections:
  88:         if section.section_status == "dropped":
  89:             continue
  90:         for sentence in section.verified_sentences:

 834: def _parse_verified_report(raw: Mapping[str, Any]) -> VerifiedReport:
 835:     _require_keys(raw, ("sections", "totals"), "verification_details.json")
 836:     if not isinstance(raw["sections"], list):
 837:         raise AuditIRSchemaError("verification_details.json: 'sections' must be a list")
 838:     sections: list[ReportSection] = []
 839:     for sec in raw["sections"]:
 840:         title = str(sec.get("title", ""))
 841:         kept_raw = sec.get("kept", []) or []
 842:         dropped_raw = sec.get("dropped", []) or []
 843:         sentences = list(
 844:             _parse_verification_sentence(s, title, "kept", i)
 845:             for i, s in enumerate(kept_raw)
 846:         )
 847:         sentences.extend(
 848:             _parse_verification_sentence(s, title, "dropped", i)
 849:             for i, s in enumerate(dropped_raw)
 850:         )
 851:         sections.append(
 852:             ReportSection(
 853:                 title=title,
 854:                 kept_count=int(sec.get("total_kept", len(kept_raw))),
 855:                 dropped_count=int(sec.get("total_dropped", len(dropped_raw))),
 856:                 total_in=int(sec.get("total_in", 0)),
 857:                 dropped_due_to_failure=int(sec.get("dropped_due_to_failure", 0)),
 858:                 sentences=tuple(sentences),
 859:             )
 860:         )
 861:     totals = raw.get("totals", {}) or {}
 862:     drop_counts = raw.get("drop_reason_counts", {}) or {}
 863:     return VerifiedReport(
 864:         sections=tuple(sections),
 865:         sentences_verified=int(totals.get("sentences_verified", 0)),
 866:         sentences_dropped=int(totals.get("sentences_dropped", 0)),
 867:         drop_reason_counts=MappingProxyType(
 868:             {str(k): int(v) for k, v in drop_counts.items()}
 869:         ),
 870:     )
